### Other {#Other}

[[\[]{.mw-editsection-bracket}[edit](/w/index.php?title=Orb:_On_the_Movements_of_the_Earth&action=edit&section=12 "Edit section: Other")[\]]{.mw-editsection-bracket}]{.mw-editsection}

The manga was featured in the music video for [Amazarashi](/wiki/Amazarashi "Amazarashi")\'s song \"1.0\" on March 30, 2022, with the video showing lyrics using [letterpress printing](/wiki/Letterpress_printing "Letterpress printing") on art from the series.^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}41[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-45)^ It was also featured in the music video for Amazarashi\'s song \"Cassiopeia Mooring\"[ ([[カシオピア係留所]{lang="ja"}]{title="Japanese-language text"}, [*Kashiopia Keiryū-sho*]{title="Hepburn transliteration"})]{style="font-weight: normal"}, released on June 30, 2022, with characters from the series and their dialogue being projected onto the [planetarium](/wiki/Planetarium "Planetarium") of the Itabashi Science and Education Museum in Tokyo.^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}42[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-46)^

## Reception {#Reception}

[[\[]{.mw-editsection-bracket}[edit](/w/index.php?title=Orb:_On_the_Movements_of_the_Earth&action=edit&section=13 "Edit section: Reception")[\]]{.mw-editsection-bracket}]{.mw-editsection}

By February 2025, the manga had over 5 million copies in circulation.^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}43[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-47)^ The manga was recommended by manga artists [Hitoshi Iwaaki](/wiki/Hitoshi_Iwaaki "Hitoshi Iwaaki") and [Shin Takahashi](/wiki/Shin_Takahashi "Shin Takahashi").^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}44[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-48)[[\[]{.cite-bracket}45[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-49)^ *Chi* was nominated for the 14th [Manga Taishō](/wiki/Manga_Taish%C5%8D "Manga Taishō") in 2021 and placed second with 67 points;^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}46[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-50)[[\[]{.cite-bracket}47[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-51)^ it was nominated for the 15th edition in 2022 and placed fifth with 59 points.^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}48[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-52)[[\[]{.cite-bracket}49[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-53)^ It was nominated for the [Next Manga Award](/wiki/Next_Manga_Award "Next Manga Award") in 2021 and placed tenth in the print category.^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}50[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-54)^ The series ranked 37th on the 2021 \"Book of the Year\" list by *[Da Vinci](/wiki/Da_Vinci_(magazine) "Da Vinci (magazine)")* magazine;^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}51[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-55)^ it ranked 21st on the 2022 list.^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}52[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-56)^ It ranked second on [Takarajimasha](/wiki/Takarajimasha "Takarajimasha")\'s *[Kono Manga ga Sugoi!](/wiki/Kono_Manga_ga_Sugoi! "Kono Manga ga Sugoi!")* 2022 list of best manga for male readers.^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}53[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-57)^ It won the Mandō Kobayashi Manga Grand Prix 2021, created by comedian and manga enthusiast [Kendo Kobayashi](/wiki/Kendo_Kobayashi "Kendo Kobayashi").^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}54[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-58)^ The manga was nominated for the 67th [Shogakukan Manga Award](/wiki/Shogakukan_Manga_Award "Shogakukan Manga Award") in the general category in 2021;^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}55[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-59)^ it was also nominated for the 68th edition in the same category in 2022.^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}56[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-60)^ The series ranked fifth on the Nationwide Bookstore Employees\' Recommended Comics of 2022.^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}57[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-61)^ The manga was nominated for the 46th [Kodansha Manga Award](/wiki/Kodansha_Manga_Award "Kodansha Manga Award") in the general category in 2022.^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}58[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-62)^ The series won the 26th [Tezuka Osamu Cultural Prize](/wiki/Tezuka_Osamu_Cultural_Prize "Tezuka Osamu Cultural Prize") in 2022.^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}59[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-63)[[\[]{.cite-bracket}60[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-64)^ The manga won the 54th [Seiun Award](/wiki/Seiun_Award "Seiun Award") in the Best Comic category in 2023.^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}61[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-65)[[\[]{.cite-bracket}62[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-66)^

## Notes {#Notes}

[[\[]{.mw-editsection-bracket}[edit](/w/index.php?title=Orb:_On_the_Movements_of_the_Earth&action=edit&section=14 "Edit section: Notes")[\]]{.mw-editsection-bracket}]{.mw-editsection}

1.  [[**[\^](#cite_ref-4)**]{.mw-cite-backlink} [The [*[kana](/wiki/Kana "Kana")*]{title="Japanese-language romanization"} \"chi\" can represent not only the [*[kanji](/wiki/Kanji "Kanji")*]{title="Japanese-language romanization"} for \"Earth; ground\" ([[地]{lang="ja"}]{title="Japanese-language text"}), but also \"wisdom; knowledge\" ([[知]{lang="ja"}]{title="Japanese-language text"}), and \"blood\" ([[血]{lang="ja"}]{title="Japanese-language text"}).^[[\[]{.cite-bracket}3[\]]{.cite-bracket}](#cite_note-3)^]{.reference-text}]{#cite_note-4}
2.  [[**[\^](#cite_ref-5)**]{.mw-cite-backlink} [While not directly mentioned, it is heavily implied through several references that the series takes place in modern-day Poland\'s borders.]{.reference-text}]{#cite_note-5}
3.  [[\^ [^***a***^](#cite_ref-EP-Staff_41-0) [^***b***^](#cite_ref-EP-Staff_41-1)]{.mw-cite-backlink} [Production staff information is taken from the ending credits of each episode.]{.reference-text}]{#cite_note-EP-Staff-41}
4.  [[\^ [^***a***^](#cite_ref-BTB_44-0) [^***b***^](#cite_ref-BTB_44-1)]{.mw-cite-backlink} [Episodes 1 and 2 premiered back-to-back.]{.reference-text}]{#cite_note-BTB-44}
